		});

<p>In this tutorial, you will learn how to build CRUD REST APIs using Spring Boot, Spring WebFlux, and MongoDB NoSQL database.</p><p><b>Before implementing this tutorial, make sure that you have installed MongoDB on your machine and MongoDB instance is running.</b></p><p>You may also be interested in&nbsp;<a href="https://www.javaguides.net/2023/01/testing-spring-webflux-reactive-crud-rest-apis-using-webtestclient.html">Testing Spring WebFlux Reactive CRUD Rest APIs using WebTestClient</a>.</p><h1 style="text-align: left;">Spring WebFlux Overview</h1><div>Spring WebFlux is a non-blocking, reactive web framework for building reactive, scalable web applications. It is part of the Spring Framework, and it is built on top of Project Reactor, which is a reactive programming library for building asynchronous, non-blocking applications.&nbsp;</div><div><br></div><div>Spring WebFlux provides support for both server-side and client-side components, and it can be used to build web applications that are reactive and scalable. It supports the creation of RESTful web services and web applications using the functional programming style, and it provides a reactive alternative to the Spring MVC web framework.&nbsp;</div><div class="google-auto-placed ap_container" style="width: 100%; height: auto; clear: both; text-align: center;"><ins data-ad-format="auto" class="adsbygoogle adsbygoogle-noablate" data-ad-client="ca-pub-5573295123036731" data-adsbygoogle-status="done" style="display: block; margin: auto; background-color: transparent; height: 280px;" data-ad-status="filled"><div id="aswift_7_host" style="border: none; height: 280px; width: 870px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; position: relative; visibility: visible; background-color: transparent; display: inline-block; overflow: visible;" tabindex="0" title="Advertisement" aria-label="Advertisement"><iframe id="aswift_7" name="aswift_7" style="left:0;position:absolute;top:0;border:0;width:870px;height:280px;" sandbox="allow-forms allow-popups allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox allow-same-origin allow-scripts allow-top-navigation-by-user-activation" width="870" height="280" frameborder="0" marginwidth="0" marginheight="0" vspace="0" hspace="0" allowtransparency="true" scrolling="no" src="./Spring Boot WebFlux MongoDB CRUD REST API Tutorial_files/ads.html" data-google-container-id="a!8" data-google-query-id="CJ2Rm8Laiv8CFQYS1QodS7gGDw" data-load-complete="true"></iframe></div></ins></div><div><br></div><div>Spring WebFlux uses a reactive stream-based model for handling requests and responses, which allows it to handle a high volume of requests with a small number of threads. Overall, Spring WebFlux is a powerful tool for building reactive, scalable web applications, and it is well-suited for use in high-concurrency environments.</div><h1 style="text-align: left;">Reactive MongoDB Driver</h1><div>Reactive MongoDB is a driver for MongoDB that is designed to support the Reactive Streams specification. It allows developers to build reactive, non-blocking applications that can work with MongoDB in a more efficient and scalable manner.&nbsp;</div><div><br></div><div>The Reactive MongoDB driver is built on top of the MongoDB Java driver, and it provides a reactive API that can be used to perform operations on MongoDB collections. It allows developers to work with MongoDB using a reactive programming model, which allows them to write asynchronous, non-blocking code that can handle a large number of concurrent operations.&nbsp;</div><div><br></div><div>Reactive MongoDB supports all the core MongoDB features, including insert, update, delete, and find operations, and it also supports aggregation, map-reduce, and other advanced features. It can be used in conjunction with other reactive libraries, such as Project Reactor or RxJava, to build scalable, reactive applications that can work with MongoDB.&nbsp;</div><div><br></div><div>Overall, Reactive MongoDB is a powerful tool for building reactive, scalable applications that can work with MongoDB, and it is well-suited for use in high-concurrency environments.</div><h1 style="text-align: left;"><span><a name="more"></a></span>1. Create Spring Boot Application</h1><div>Let's create a Spring boot application using <a href="https://start.spring.io/" target="_blank">Spring Intializr</a>.</div><div><br></div><div>Refer to the below screenshot to enter the details while generating the Spring boot project using&nbsp;<a href="https://start.spring.io/" target="_blank">Spring Intializr</a>:</div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhAl4PkU_g9bggCD4httsmPzZ1YTEkwsXhMgOmhirlvd1H89mauGbJFSd-GidNp6A7TJGBNa9-WnxrQN2_yq-6Wt5JqGzLi0pXXmquZJRq7tgvFWfnFwEKW0otyBSKukoH7xtrwiPZ0lPcJf--QE0iwZ_02VWp_JLIDkc1GA39PWcEnGKdVX-16o391/s2528/Screenshot%202023-01-03%20at%2010.31.39%20PM.png" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" data-original-height="1512" data-original-width="2528" src="./Spring Boot WebFlux MongoDB CRUD REST API Tutorial_files/Screenshot 2023-01-03 at 10.31.39 PM.png"></a></div><div>Note that we are using Spring WebFlux, MongoDB Reactive, and Lombok libraries.</div><div><br></div><div>Here is the complete pom.xml file for your reference:</div><div class="google-auto-placed ap_container" style="width: 100%; Project Structure</h1><div>Refer to the below screenshot to create the packing or project structure for the application:</div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEgwOrm6m-hovjUF48LR0XeAGECAPAskiM1M33UuqwR8ayHVQV-m1IYv5DfZmsBkA3M80wOEOFva1PDN0R7FzCH7BnJWmTK5k5j6WR4aTJ6PhPl3JSZ9xvm6sAkHGw-_p-mOH0n7ZEz-rgCgOrO_x-uu9K-z52I9UqGl0-RoJ9ZwR_WnHn7fWCCXUrhj/s1264/Screenshot%202023-01-03%20at%2010.41.03%20PM.png" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" data-original-height="1264" data-original-width="1178" height="640" src="./Spring Boot WebFlux MongoDB CRUD REST API Tutorial_files/Screenshot 2023-01-03 at 10.41.03 PM.png" width="596"></a></div><h1 style="text-align: left;">3. Configure MongoDB</h1><div>You can configure MongoDB by simply adding the following property to the application.properties file:</div><div><pre class="notranslate" style="border-radius: 6px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #24292f; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 13.6px; line-height: 1.45; margin-bottom: 16px; margin-top: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; padding: 16px;"><code style="background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border-radius: 6px; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: visible; padding: 0px; word-break: normal;" class="hljs ini"><span class="hljs-attr">spring.data.mongodb.uri</span>=mongodb://localhost:<span class="hljs-number">27017</span>/ems</code></pre></div><div>Spring Boot will read this configuration on startup and automatically configure the data source.</div><h1 style="text-align: left;">4. Create Domain Class</h1><div>Let's create an <i>Employee</i> MongoDB document and add the following content to it:</div><div><pre class="notranslate" style="border-radius: 6px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #24292f; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 13.6px; line-height: 1.45; margin-bottom: 16px; margin-top: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; padding: 16px;"><code style="background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border-radius: 6px; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: visible; padding: 0px; word-break: normal;" class="hljs kotlin"><span class="hljs-keyword">package</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.entity;

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> lombok.Getter;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> lombok.Setter;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> org.springframework.<span class="hljs-keyword">data</span>.<span class="hljs-keyword">annotation</span>.Id;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> org.springframework.<span class="hljs-keyword">data</span>.mongodb.core.mapping.Document;

<span class="hljs-meta">@Getter</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">@Setter</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">@NoArgsConstructor</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">@AllArgsConstructor</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">@Document(value = <span class="hljs-meta-string">"employees"</span>)</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-class"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">Employee</span> </span>{

    <span class="hljs-meta">@Id</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> String id;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> String firstName;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> String lastName;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> String email;
}</code></pre></div><div>Note that we have given MongoDB collection name -&nbsp;<i>employees</i>.</div><h1 style="text-align: left;">5. Creating Repository - EmployeeRepository</h1><div>Next, were going to create the data access layer which will be used to access the MongoDB database.</div><div><br></div><div>Let's create an <i>EmployeeRepository</i> interface and add the following content to it:</div><div><pre class="notranslate" style="border-radius: 6px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #24292f; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 13.6px; line-height: 1.45; margin-bottom: 16px; margin-top: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; padding: 16px;"><code style="background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border-radius: 6px; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: visible; padding: 0px; word-break: normal;" class="hljs css"><span class="hljs-selector-tag">package</span> <span class="hljs-selector-tag">net</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.javaguides</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.springbootwebfluxdemo</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.repository</span>;

<span class="hljs-selector-tag">import</span> <span class="hljs-selector-tag">net</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.javaguides</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.springbootwebfluxdemo</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.entity</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.Employee</span>;
<span class="hljs-selector-tag">import</span> <span class="hljs-selector-tag">org</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.springframework</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.data</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.repository</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.reactive</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.ReactiveCrudRepository</span>;

<span class="hljs-selector-tag">public</span> <span class="hljs-selector-tag">interface</span> <span class="hljs-selector-tag">EmployeeRepository</span> <span class="hljs-selector-tag">extends</span> <span class="hljs-selector-tag">ReactiveCrudRepository</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-selector-tag">Employee</span>, <span class="hljs-selector-tag">String</span>&gt; {
}</code></pre></div><div>The <i>EmployeeRepository</i> interface extends from <i>ReactiveMongoRepository</i> which exposes various CRUD methods on the Document. Spring Boot automatically plugs in an implementation of this interface called <i>SimpleReactiveMongoRepository</i> at runtime.</div><div><br></div><div>So you get all the CRUD methods on the Document readily available to you without needing to write any code.</div><h1 style="text-align: left;">6. Create EmployeeMapper - Map Entity to Dto and Vice Versa</h1><div>Let's create <i>EmployeeMapper</i> class to map an entity to Dto and vice versa:</div><div><pre class="notranslate" style="border-radius: 6px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #24292f; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 13.6px; line-height: 1.45; margin-bottom: 16px; margin-top: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; padding: 16px;"><code style="background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border-radius: 6px; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: visible; padding: 0px; word-break: normal;" class="hljs typescript">package net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.mapper;

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.dto.EmployeeDto;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.entity.Employee;

<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-class"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">EmployeeMapper</span> </span>{

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> EmployeeDto <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-title">mapToEmployeeDto</span>(<span class="hljs-params">Employee employee</span>)</span>{
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> EmployeeDto(
                employee.getId(),
                employee.getFirstName(),
                employee.getLastName(),
                employee.getEmail()
        );
    }

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> Employee <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-title">mapToEmployee</span>(<span class="hljs-params">EmployeeDto employeeDto</span>)</span>{
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> Employee(
                employeeDto.getId(),
                employeeDto.getFirstName(),
                employeeDto.getLastName(),
                employeeDto.getEmail()
        );
    }
}</code></pre></div><h1 style="text-align: left;">7. Create Service Layer</h1><h2 style="text-align: left;">EmployeeService Interface</h2><div>Let's create an <i>EmployeeService</i> interface and add below CRUD methods to it:</div><div><pre class="notranslate" style="border-radius: 6px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #24292f; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 13.6px; line-height: 1.45; margin-bottom: 16px; margin-top: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; padding: 16px;"><code style="background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border-radius: 6px; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: visible; padding: 0px; word-break: normal;" class="hljs java"><span class="hljs-keyword">package</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.service;

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.dto.EmployeeDto;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> reactor.core.publisher.Flux;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> reactor.core.publisher.Mono;

<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-class"><span class="hljs-keyword">interface</span> <span class="hljs-title">EmployeeService</span> </span>{
    <span class="hljs-function">Mono&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; <span class="hljs-title">saveEmployee</span><span class="hljs-params">(EmployeeDto employeeDto)</span></span>;

    <span class="hljs-function">Mono&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; <span class="hljs-title">getEmployee</span><span class="hljs-params">(String employeeId)</span></span>;

    <span class="hljs-function">Flux&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; <span class="hljs-title">getAllEmployees</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span></span>;

    <span class="hljs-function">Mono&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; <span class="hljs-title">updateEmployee</span><span class="hljs-params">(EmployeeDto employeeDto, String employeeId)</span></span>;

    <span class="hljs-function">Mono&lt;Void&gt; <span class="hljs-title">deleteEmployee</span><span class="hljs-params">(String employeeId)</span></span>;
}</code></pre></div><h2 style="text-align: left;">EmployeeServiceImpl class</h2><div>Let's create <i>EmployeeServiceImpl</i> class that implements the <i>EmployeeService</i> interface and its methods:</div><div><br></div><div><pre class="notranslate" style="border-radius: 6px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #24292f; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 13.6px; line-height: 1.45; margin-bottom: 16px; margin-top: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; padding: 16px;"><code style="background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border-radius: 6px; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: visible; padding: 0px; word-break: normal;" class="hljs typescript">package net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.service.impl;

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.dto.EmployeeDto;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.entity.Employee;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.mapper.EmployeeMapper;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.repository.EmployeeRepository;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.service.EmployeeService;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> reactor.core.publisher.Flux;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> reactor.core.publisher.Mono;

<span class="hljs-meta">@Service</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">@AllArgsConstructor</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-class"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">EmployeeServiceImpl</span> <span class="hljs-title">implements</span> <span class="hljs-title">EmployeeService</span> </span>{

    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> EmployeeRepository employeeRepository;

    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> Mono&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-title">saveEmployee</span>(<span class="hljs-params">EmployeeDto employeeDto</span>)</span> {
        Employee employee = EmployeeMapper.mapToEmployee(employeeDto);
        Mono&lt;Employee&gt; savedEmployee = employeeRepository.save(employee);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> savedEmployee
                .map((employeeEntity) -&gt; EmployeeMapper.mapToEmployeeDto(employeeEntity));
    }

    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> Mono&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-title">getEmployee</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">String</span> employeeId</span>)</span> {
        Mono&lt;Employee&gt; employeeMono = employeeRepository.findById(employeeId);
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> employeeMono.map((employee -&gt; EmployeeMapper.mapToEmployeeDto(employee)));
    }

    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> Flux&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-title">getAllEmployees</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>)</span> {

        Flux&lt;Employee&gt; employeeFlux  = employeeRepository.findAll();
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> employeeFlux
                .map((employee) -&gt; EmployeeMapper.mapToEmployeeDto(employee))
                .switchIfEmpty(Flux.empty());
    }

    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> Mono&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-title">updateEmployee</span>(<span class="hljs-params">EmployeeDto employeeDto, <span class="hljs-built_in">String</span> employeeId</span>)</span> {

        Mono&lt;Employee&gt; employeeMono = employeeRepository.findById(employeeId);

        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> employeeMono.flatMap((existingEmployee) -&gt; {
            existingEmployee.setFirstName(employeeDto.getFirstName());
            existingEmployee.setLastName(employeeDto.getLastName());
            existingEmployee.setEmail(employeeDto.getEmail());
            <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> employeeRepository.save(existingEmployee);
        }).map((employee -&gt; EmployeeMapper.mapToEmployeeDto(employee)));
    }

    <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> Mono&lt;Void&gt; <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-title">deleteEmployee</span>(<span class="hljs-params"><span class="hljs-built_in">String</span> employeeId</span>)</span> {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> employeeRepository.deleteById(employeeId);
    }
}</code></pre></div><h1 style="text-align: left;">8. Create Controller Layer - Reactive REST APIs</h1><div>Lets write the APIs that will be exposed to the clients. Let's create an <i>EmployeeController</i>&nbsp;with the following contents:</div><div><pre class="notranslate" style="border-radius: 6px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #24292f; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; font-size: 13.6px; line-height: 1.45; margin-bottom: 16px; margin-top: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: auto; padding: 16px;"><code style="background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border-radius: 6px; border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; font-family: ui-monospace, SFMono-Regular, &quot;SF Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;Liberation Mono&quot;, monospace; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; overflow-wrap: normal; overflow: visible; padding: 0px; word-break: normal;" class="hljs kotlin"><span class="hljs-keyword">package</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.controller;

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.dto.EmployeeDto;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> net.javaguides.springbootwebfluxdemo.service.EmployeeService;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> org.springframework.web.bind.<span class="hljs-keyword">annotation</span>.*;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> reactor.core.publisher.Flux;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> reactor.core.publisher.Mono;

<span class="hljs-meta">@RestController</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">@RequestMapping(<span class="hljs-meta-string">"api/employees"</span>)</span>
<span class="hljs-meta">@AllArgsConstructor</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-class"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">EmployeeController</span> </span>{

    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> EmployeeService employeeService;

    <span class="hljs-meta">@PostMapping</span>
    <span class="hljs-meta">@ResponseStatus(value = HttpStatus.CREATED)</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> Mono&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; saveEmployee(<span class="hljs-meta">@RequestBody</span> EmployeeDto employeeDto){
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> employeeService.saveEmployee(employeeDto);
    }

    <span class="hljs-meta">@GetMapping(<span class="hljs-meta-string">"{id}"</span>)</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> Mono&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; getEmployee(<span class="hljs-meta">@PathVariable(<span class="hljs-meta-string">"id"</span>)</span> String employeeId){
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> employeeService.getEmployee(employeeId);
    }

    <span class="hljs-meta">@GetMapping</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> Flux&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; getAllEmployees(){
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> employeeService.getAllEmployees();
    }

    <span class="hljs-meta">@PutMapping(<span class="hljs-meta-string">"{id}"</span>)</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> Mono&lt;EmployeeDto&gt; updateEmployee(<span class="hljs-meta">@RequestBody</span> EmployeeDto employeeDto,
                                            <span class="hljs-meta">@PathVariable(<span class="hljs-meta-string">"id"</span>)</span> String employeeId){
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> employeeService.updateEmployee(employeeDto, employeeId);
    }

    <span class="hljs-meta">@DeleteMapping(<span class="hljs-meta-string">"{id}"</span>)</span>
    <span class="hljs-meta">@ResponseStatus(value = HttpStatus.NO_CONTENT)</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> Mono&lt;<span class="hljs-built_in">Void</span>&gt; deleteEmployee(<span class="hljs-meta">@PathVariable(<span class="hljs-meta-string">"id"</span>)</span> String employeeId){
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> employeeService.deleteEmployee(employeeId);
    }
}</code></pre></div><div>Note that all the controller endpoints return a Publisher in the form of a <i>Flux</i> or a <i>Mono.</i></div><h1 style="text-align: left;">Testing Reactive CRUD REST APIs using Postman Client</h1><h2 style="text-align: left;">Create Employee REST API:&nbsp;</h2><div class="separator" style="clear: both;
